ENTRY_POINT
_calculatePrizesAwardable(uint256[],bytes32,IDrawBeacon.Draw[],uint64[][],IPrizeDistributionBuffer.PrizeDistribution[])
ENTRY_POINT
NEW VARIABLE _prizesAwardable = new uint256[](_normalizedUserBalances.length)
NEW VARIABLE _prizeCounts = new uint256[][](_normalizedUserBalances.length)
NEW VARIABLE drawIndex = 0
BEGIN_LOOP
IF_LOOP drawIndex < _draws.length
END_LOOP
NEW VARIABLE totalUserPicks = _calculateNumberOfUserPicks(_prizeDistributions[drawIndex],_normalizedUserBalances[drawIndex])
EXPRESSION prizeCounts = abi.encode(_prizeCounts)
EXPRESSION (_prizesAwardable[drawIndex],_prizeCounts[drawIndex]) = _calculate(_draws[drawIndex].winningRandomNumber,totalUserPicks,_userRandomNumber,_pickIndicesForDraws[drawIndex],_prizeDistributions[drawIndex])
EXPRESSION prizesAwardable = _prizesAwardable
EXPRESSION drawIndex ++
IF_LOOP drawIndex < _draws.length
RETURN (prizesAwardable,prizeCounts)

EXPRESSION maxWinningTierIndex = tiersIndex

END_LOOP

_createBitMasks(IPrizeDistributionBuffer.PrizeDistribution)
ENTRY_POINT
NEW VARIABLE masks = new uint256[](_prizeDistribution.matchCardinality)
NEW VARIABLE _bitRangeMaskValue = (2 ** _prizeDistribution.bitRangeSize) - 1
NEW VARIABLE maskIndex = 0
BEGIN_LOOP
IF_LOOP maskIndex < _prizeDistribution.matchCardinality
NEW VARIABLE _matchIndexOffset = uint256(maskIndex) * uint256(_prizeDistribution.bitRangeSize)
END_LOOP
EXPRESSION masks[maskIndex] = _bitRangeMaskValue << _matchIndexOffset
RETURN masks

ENTRY_POINT
_numberOfPrizesForIndex(uint8,uint256)
ENTRY_POINT
NEW VARIABLE bitRangeDecimal = 2 ** uint256(_bitRangeSize)
NEW VARIABLE numberOfPrizesForIndex = bitRangeDecimal ** _prizeTierIndex
BEGIN_LOOP
IF_LOOP _prizeTierIndex > 0
END_LOOP
EXPRESSION numberOfPrizesForIndex -= bitRangeDecimal ** (_prizeTierIndex - 1)
EXPRESSION _prizeTierIndex --
IF_LOOP _prizeTierIndex > 0
RETURN numberOfPrizesForIndex

ENTRY_POINT
_calculateTierIndex(uint256,uint256,uint256[])
ENTRY_POINT
NEW VARIABLE numberOfMatches = 0
NEW VARIABLE masksLength = uint8(_masks.length)
NEW VARIABLE matchIndex = 0
BEGIN_LOOP
IF_LOOP matchIndex < masksLength
NEW VARIABLE mask = _masks[matchIndex]
END_LOOP
RETURN masksLength - numberOfMatches
IF (_randomNumberThisPick & mask) != (_winningRandomNumber & mask)
END_IF
EXPRESSION numberOfMatches ++
RETURN masksLength - numberOfMatches
EXPRESSION matchIndex ++
IF_LOOP matchIndex < masksLength
